# Book 1 French Translation QA

Date: 2026-06-30
Scope: complete Book 1, `ch1` through `ch11b`, EN/FR pairs before corrections.
Status: every row was validated and then applied to the FR sources. This report remains the correction checklist, not the current state of the texts.

## Method

- Compared canonical English `messages` and source French messages for the 12 Book 1 chapters.
- Targeted calques already documented in `docs/translation-fr.md`.
- Scanned first-person dialogue tags, `Yeah` translated as `Oui`, straight quotes, calqued dialogue punctuation, overly precise units, and several literal English turns of phrase.
- Each row references an existing `messageId` and documents the correction validated before source edits.

## Severity Guide

- `High`: correction recommended before considering Book 1 properly reread in French.
- `Medium`: likely issue with naturalness, register, or consistency; sweep after high-severity items.
- `Low`: editorial improvement or style normalization, often dependent on final punctuation choices.

## Cross-Cutting Notes

- Chapters `ch10`, `ch11a`, and `ch11b` concentrate many straight quotes and dialogue punctuation fixes.
- First-person dialogue tags remain the main risk outside typography: several forms such as `je lui demande`, `lui demandé-je`, `crié-je`, or `commencé-je` should be reformulated rather than mechanically corrected.
- `Oui` is not forbidden, but `registre-yeah` rows must be reread with the speaker's voice: Barry, Daren, and Hadrik often call for `Ouais`, while Kate, Rose, or Flower may keep `Oui` depending on the scene.
- Present-tense narration is preserved; this pass does not propose a general conversion to literary past tense.
